when you say she's a programmer , she did do some , but the real thing is to have said the future is going to be much , much more than this .	當你說她是程式設計師 , 她確實做了一些事情 , 但真正的事情是 , 未來會變得越來越多 。
now , a hundred years later , this guy comes along , alan turing , and in 1936 , and invents the computer all over again .	幾百年後 , 這個人在1936年 , 發明了電腦 。
now , of course , babbage's machine was entirely mechanical .	當然 , 貝爾的機器完全機械 。
turing's machine was entirely theoretical .	turs機器完全是理論 。
both of these guys were coming from a mathematical perspective , but turing told us something very important .	這些人都是從數學角度來看的 , 但我們非常重要的 。
he laid down the mathematical foundations for computer science , and said , " it doesn't matter how you make a computer . "	他把數學基金給電腦學基金 , 說: 「 不論你如何製造電腦 。 」
it doesn't matter if your computer's mechanical , like babbage's was , or electronic , like computers are today , or perhaps in the future , cells , or , again , mechanical again , once we get into nanotechnology .	不管你是電腦的機械技術 , 像是bage的電腦機械 , 或電子 , 像是bage的機械 , 或電子 , 只要我們進入奈米科技 。
we could go back to babbage's machine and just make it tiny . all those things are computers .	我們可以回到巴比的機器 , 讓它微小 , 所有東西都是電腦 。
there is in a sense a computing essence .	有一種計算機率 。
this is called the church–turing thesis .	這叫做教堂 。
and so suddenly , you get this link where you say this thing babbage had built really was a computer .	突然間 , 你得到這個連結 , 說這東西是電腦 。
in fact , it was capable of doing everything we do today with computers , only really slowly .	事實上 , 只要慢慢地使用電腦 , 只是真的很慢 。
to give you an idea of how slowly , it had about 1k of memory .	給你一個想法慢慢地 , 它有1k記憶 。
it used punch cards , which were being fed in , and it ran about 10 , 000 times slower the first zx81 .	它使用punch卡片 , 它會用punch卡片 , 它會用punch卡片 , 它會用punch卡片 , 大約10000倍 。
it did have a ram pack .	它有一支支援機 。
you could add on a lot of extra memory if you wanted to .	你可以增加很多額外的記憶 。
so , where does that bring us today ?	所以 , 今天我們來到哪裡呢 ?
so there are plans .	所以 , 有計畫 。
over in swindon , the science museum archives , there are hundreds of plans and thousands of pages of notes written by charles babbage about this analytical engine .	在瑞典博物館 , 科學博物館有數以千計的數以千計的數以千計的數以千計的數以千計 。
one of those is a set of plans that we call plan 28 , and that is also the name of a charity that i started with doron swade , who was the curator of computing at the science museum , and also the person who drove the project to build a difference engine , and our plan is to build it .	其中之一是2008年 , 也是我在科學博物館的名字 , 這也是我們所謂的 「 慈善計畫 」 的計畫 。
here in south kensington , we will build the analytical engine .	在南韓 , 我們會建造一個分析引擎 。
the project has a number of parts to it .	這個計畫有數量的部分 。
one was the scanning of babbage's archive .	一個是babbage的掃描 。
that's been done . the second is now the study of all of those plans to determine what to build .	這已經完成了 。 第二個研究是所有這些計畫的研究 , 來決定該怎麼做 。
the third part is a computer simulation of that machine , and the last part is to physically build it at the science museum .	第三件是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 。
when it's built , you'll finally be able to understand how a computer works , because rather than having a tiny chip in front of you , you've got to look at this humongous thing and say , " ah , i see the memory operating , i see the cpu operating , i hear it operating . i probably smell it operating . "	當它運作時 , 你就可以了解電腦運作的運作方式 , 因為在你面前 , 你可能聞到它的運作 , 我聽到它運作 , 我會聽到它運作 , 我會聽到它運作 , 我聽到它運作 , 我會聽到它運作 。
but in between that we're going to do a simulation .	但在我們要做模擬時 ,
babbage himself wrote , he said , as soon as the analytical engine exists , it will surely guide the future course of science .	貝爾夫寫了 , 他說: 「 科技科學 」 , 它會確保未來的未來科學 。
of course , he never built it , because he was always fiddling with new plans , but when it did get built , of course , in the 1940s , everything changed .	當然 , 他從來沒有建構 , 因為他一直在1940年代 , 一切都改變了 。

in this accessible talk from tedxboston , richard resnick shows how cheap and fast genome sequencing is about to turn health care upside down .	在tedxboston的演講中 , 理查•安德斯頓 , 理查•安德森林士頓 , 理查•安德森林士頓 , 理查•安德森 , 理查•安德斯頓 , 理查•安德斯頓 , 理查•安德森林士頓
dna , biotech , health care , science , technology	dna、生物科技、科學、科技 。
richard resnick: welcome to the genomic revolution	理查德•雷斯尼克:歡迎到基因組革命 。
ladies and gentlemen , i present to you the human genome .	各位先生女士 , 我給各位看人類基因組 。
chromosome one , top left .	染色體是左邊
bottom right are the sex chromosomes .	底部是性染色體 。
women have two copies of that big x chromosome ; men have the x and , of course , that small copy of the y .	女性有兩個共同的x染色體x染色體x染色體x染色體x染色體x染色體x染色體x染色體
sorry boys , but it's just a tiny little thing that makes you different .	抱歉男孩 , 但它只是一個小小東西 , 讓你不一樣 。
so if you zoom in on this genome , then what you see , of course , is this double helix structure the code of life spelled out with these four biochemical letters , or we call them bases , right: a , c , g and t .	如果你放大這個基因組 , 你看到的 , 就是這個基因組 , 我們稱它們為基礎: 「 四個生物化學字母 」 , 或我們稱它們為 「 基礎 」 。
how many are there in the human genome ? three billion .	在人類基因組中有多少 ? 三十億 。
is that a big number ?	這是個巨大數字嗎 ?
well , everybody can throw around big numbers .	每個人都可以丟大數字 。
but in fact , if i were to place one base on each pixel of this 1280 by 800 resolution screen , we would need 3 , 000 screens to take a look at the genome .	但事實上 , 如果我要把一個基礎應用在20800個螢幕上 , 我們需要3 , 000個螢幕 , 我們需要3 , 000個螢幕 , 看看基因組 。
so it's really quite big .	這真的很大 。
and perhaps because of its size , a group of people all , by the way , with y chromosomes decided they would want to sequence it .	或許是因為它大小 , 一群人 , 和y染色體 , 牠們會想要追蹤它 。
and so 15 years , actually , and about four billion dollars later , the genome was sequenced and published .	15年後 , 基因序列出版了 。
in 2003 , the final version was published , and they keep working on it .	2003年 , 在2003年 , 最後版版的版本 , 他們繼續努力 。
that was all done on a machine that looks like this .	這一切都在機器上看起來像這樣 。
it costs about a dollar for each base a very slow way of doing it .	它花了一美元 , 每一塊錢都要花一點錢 。
well folks , i'm here to tell you that the world has completely changed and none of you know about it .	嗯 , 我在這裡告訴各位 , 世界已經完全改變了 , 沒有人知道 。

daniel kraft demos his marrow miner a new device that quickly harvests lifesaving bone marrow with minimal pain to the donor . he emphasizes that the adult stem cells found in bone marrow can be used to treat many terminal conditions , from parkinson's to heart disease .	丹尼爾•克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克雷克拉克拉克獎 , 他強調 , 讓它能被用來治療許多常常疾病 。 他強調到捐贈者 , 來治療許多精神疾病 。

daniel kraft invents a better way to harvest bone marrow	丹尼爾•克雷克拉ft發明了一個更好的方法 , 來捕捉船骨 。
so i am a pediatric cancer doctor and stemcell researcher at stanford university where my clinical focus has been bone marrow transplantation .	我是骨髓移植手術 , 研究人員在史丹佛大學 , 我的臨床專注是骨髓移植手術 。
now , inspired by jill bolte taylor last year , i didn't bring a human brain , but i did bring a liter of bone marrow .	最近年來 , 我沒有帶出一個人腦袋 , 但是我拿了一座紅色的骨髓 。
and bone marrow is actually what we use to save the lives of tens of thousands of patients , most of whom have advanced malignancies like leukemia and lymphoma and some other diseases .	骨髓實際上是我們用來拯救生命的數千個病患 , 大部分的哺乳類和其他疾病 。
so , a few years ago , i'm doing my transplant fellowship at stanford .	幾年前 , 我在史丹佛大學 。
i'm in the operating room . we have bob here , who is a volunteer donor .	我在手術室裡 , 我們有一位志願者 。
we're sending his marrow across the country to save the life of a child with leukemia .	我們把他的火箭送出他的火箭 , 拯救了美國人的生命 。
so actually how do we harvest this bone marrow ?	那麼 , 我們如何把這骨髓帶到骨髓呢 ?
well we have a whole o . r . team , general anesthesia , nurses , and another doctor across from me .	嗯 , 我們有了一間全部的醫生 , 包括麻醉、護士和其他醫生 。
bob's on the table , and we take this sort of small needle , you know , not too big .	博士在桌子上 , 我們拿著這個小小的需求 , 不太大 。
and the way we do this is we basically place this through the soft tissue , and kind of punch it into the hard bone , into the tuchus that's a technical term and aspirate about 10 mls of bone marrow out , each time , with a syringe .	我們所做的是 , 把這個軟體組織起來 , 用軟體組織起來 , 將它轉化為骨髓 , 每次 , 大約10個骨頭骨髓 , 每次 , 用軟組織 。
and hand it off to the nurse . she squirts it into a tin .	牠把牠放進去 , 牠把牠放進一間 。
hands it back to me . and we do that again and again .	再一次 , 我再次再次重覆 。
about 200 times usually .	大約200倍 。
and by the end of this my arm is sore , i've got a callus on my hand , let alone bob , whose rear end looks something more like this , like swiss cheese .	最後 , 我的手臂上有了一支手 , 讓單單單單單單單單 , 像瑞士斯一樣 。
so i'm thinking , you know , this procedure hasn't changed in about 40 years .	所以我在想 , 你知道的 , 這段程序已經改變了40年 。
and there is probably a better way to do this .	可能有更好的方法 。
so i thought of a minimally invasive approach , and a new device that we call the marrow miner .	因此我想到了一個新設備 , 我們稱之為 「 火箭礦坑 」 。
and the marrow miner , the way it works is shown here .	而火箭礦工 , 它的工作是呈現出來的 。
our standard seethrough patient .	我們的標準病人 。
instead of entering the bone dozens of times , we enter just once , into the front of the hip or the back of the hip .	不是進入前面的前面 , 而是進入前面 , 進入前面 , 進入前面 , 而是進入前面 。
and we have a flexible , powered catheter with a special wire loop tip that stays inside the crunchy part of the marrow and follows the contours of the hip , as it moves around .	我們有彈性 , 用特殊的線路線路 , 讓它移動到處 。
so it enables you to very rapidly aspirate , or suck out , rich bone marrow very quickly through one hole .	所以它可以讓你快速迅速地跳動 , 很快就在一個洞內 。
we can do multiple passes through that same entry .	我們可以透過相同的乘法來做多次 。
and , so , very quickly , bob can just get one puncture , local anesthesia , and do this harvest as an outpatient .	很快的 , 波布可以只能得到一個創傷、當地的麻醉 , 不管是哪裡 , 就這樣 。
so i did a few prototypes . i got a small little grant at stanford .	所以我做了幾個原型 , 我在史丹佛大學做了一些原型 。
and played around with this a little bit .	用這一點點 。
and our team members developed this technology .	我們的團隊成員開發了這項技術 。
and eventually we got two large animals , and pig studies .	最後我們有兩個大型動物 , 以及豬研究 。
and we found , to our surprise , that we not only got bone marrow out , but we got 10 times the stem cell activity in the marrow from the marrow miner , compared to the normal device .	我們發現 , 我們發現 , 對於一般的裝置 , 我們發現的 , 不僅是骨髓 , 而是有十倍的幹細胞活動 , 比一般裝置還要有十倍 。
this device was just fda approved in the last year .	這個裝置只是fda應用在過去一年
here is a live patient . you can see it following the flexible curves around .	這裡是病人 , 你可以看到它追蹤著有彈性的曲線 。
there will be two passes here , in the same patient , from the same hole .	這裡有兩位相同的病人 , 同一個洞 。
this was done under local anesthesia , as an outpatient .	這是在當地的亞洲 , 身為一個獨裁者 。
and we got , again , about three to six times more stem cells than the standard approach done on the same patient .	再次 , 我們有三到六倍的幹細胞 , 比標準方法更幹細胞 。
so why should you care ? bone marrow is a very rich source of adult stem cells .	為什麼你要關心 ? 骨髓是個非常豐富的成年人幹細胞 。
you all know about embryonic stem cells .	你們都知道胚胎幹細胞 。
they've got great potential but haven't yet entered clinical trials .	他們有很大的潛力 , 但還沒有進入臨床試驗 。
adult stem cells are throughout our body , including the bloodforming stem cells in our bone marrow , which we've been using as a form of stemcell therapy for over 40 years .	成年人幹細胞在身體內 , 包含在骨髓內部的幹細胞 , 包括在骨髓中 , 包含了我們骨髓的幹細胞 , 包含了四十年內的幹細胞 。
in the last decade there's been an explosion of use of bone marrow stem cells to treat the patient's other diseases such as heart disease , vascular disease , orthopedics , tissue engineering , even in neurology to treat parkinson's and diabetes .	在過去的十年內 , 骨髓幹細胞可以治療病人的其他疾病 , 像是心臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病、肺臟病 , 甚至是神經細胞治療病人的疾病 。
we've just come out , we're commercializing , this year , generation 2 . 0 of the marrow miner .	我們剛剛出去 , 今年 , 一代2.0.0.0.
the hope is that this gets more stem cells out , which translates to better outcomes .	希望是 , 更好的結果會變得更好 。
it may encourage more people to sign up to be potential livesaving bone marrow donors .	可能鼓勵更多人願意冒險更多的人 , 可以鼓勵更多人來追求潛力的骨髓捐贈 。
it may even enable you to bank your own marrow stem cells , when you're younger and healthier , to use in the future should you need it .	甚至可以讓你能把你的心胸放進去 , 只要你更年輕、更健康、更年輕、更健康 , 需要它 。
and ultimately and here's a picture of our bone marrow transplant survivors , who come together for a reunion each year at stanford .	最後 , 這是我們骨髓移植手術的照片 , 每年在史丹佛 。
hopefully this technology will let us have more of these survivors in the future .	希望科技能讓我們有更多的生存者 。
physicist and surfer garrett lisi presents a controversial new model of the universe that just maybe answers all the big questions . if nothing else , it's the most beautiful 8dimensional model of elementary particles and forces you've ever seen .	物理學家和波斯維爾•格雷特雷特物理學家 , 和你所見過的最美麗的8d物理學家 , 和你所見過的任何東西 。
physics , science , technology	物理學、科學、科學 。
garrett lisi on his theory of everything	格雷特雷特在他的理論上看到了一切 。
whoa , dude . check out those killer equations . sweet .	沒錯 , 看看那些殺方方程式 。
actually , for the next 18 minutes i'm going to do the best i can to describe the beauty of particle physics without equations .	事實上 , 接下來18分鐘 , 我要做最好的 , 我可以描述美麗的粒子物理不平等 。
it turns out there's a lot we can learn from coral .	結果發現 , 很多我們可以從珊瑚身上學到 。
coral is a very beautiful and unusual animal .	珊瑚是非常美且不尋常的動物 。
each coral head consists of thousand of individual polyps .	每個珊瑚的頭包含數千個個體 。
these polyps are continually budding and branching into genetically identical neighbors .	這些蜜蜂會不斷被遺傳到基因上 , 牠們會不斷地被遺傳到基因上 。
if we imagine this to be a hyperintelligent coral , we can single out an individual and ask him a reasonable question .	如果我們想像這是個高智利的問題 , 我們就可以單單一個個別問他一個問題 。
we can ask how exactly he got to be in this particular location compared to his neighbors if it was just chance , or destiny , or what ?	我們可以問他如何在這個特定的位置 , 可以問他在這個特定位置的位置 , 還是有機會 ?
now , after admonishing us for turning the temperature up too high , he would tell us that our question was completely stupid .	現在 , 要告訴我們問題是完全愚蠢的 。
these corals can be quite kind of mean , you see , and i have surfing scars to prove that .	這些珊瑚都可以很有意義 , 我有很大膽的看法 。
but this polyp would continue and tell us that his neighbors were quite clearly identical copies of him .	但這波普會持續告訴我們 , 他的鄰居是非常明顯的同事 。
that he was in all these other locations as well , but experiencing them as separate individuals .	他在其他的位置都在這些其他位置 , 但在這些其他地位上 , 會讓它們分裂 。
for a coral , branching into different copies is the most natural thing in the world .	對珊瑚而言 , 世界中最自然的東西 。
unlike us , a hyperintelligent coral would be uniquely prepared to understand quantum mechanics .	不像我們 , 大量子力學 , 很不可思議的 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics very accurately describes how our universe works .	量子力學的數學是量子力學的數學 , 量子力學非常準確描述我們的宇宙 。
and it tells us our reality is continually branching into different possibilities , just like a coral .	它告訴我們我們的現實是持續不斷地擴展到不同的可能性 , 就像珊瑚 。
it's a weird thing for us humans to wrap our minds around , since we only ever get to experience one possibility .	對人類來說 , 很奇怪的是 , 因為我們只能經歷一個可能性 。
this quantum weirdness was first described by erwin schrödinger and his cat .	這種量子量子的描述是雙胞胎和他的貓 。
the cat likes this version better .	像是這個版本更好 。
in this setup , schrödinger is in a box with a radioactive sample that , by the laws of quantum mechanics , branches into a state in which it is radiated and a state in which it is not .	在這個設置中 , 法律量子力學的法律量子力學 , 用量子力學的原則 , 來源於量子力學的原則 , 而不是 。
in the branch in which the sample radiates , it sets off a trigger that releases poison and schrödinger is dead .	在這個區域中 , 它會釋放出毒劑和呼吸器 , 它會釋放出毒劑和作者 。
but in the other branch of reality , he remains alive .	但在其他的情況下 , 他仍然活著 。
these realities are experienced separately by each individual .	這些真實體驗分離每個人 。
as far as either can tell , the other one doesn't exist .	就算不存在 , 其他的情況也不存在 。
this seems weird to us , because each of us only experiences an individual existence , and we don't get to see other branches .	這似乎很奇怪 , 因為我們每個人都只有體驗一個獨立的體驗 , 因為每個人都只有經驗 , 因為每個人的體驗都是獨立的 。
it's as if each of us , like schrödinger here , are a kind of coral branching into different possibilities .	像schroldschr一樣 , 他們是種種植入不同的可能性 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics tells us this is how the world works at tiny scales .	量子力學的數學量子力學告訴我們這個世界是如何運作的 。
it can be summed up in a single sentence: everything that can happen , does .	它可以在單一句子:所有事情都能發生 。
but this does not mean everything happens .	但這並不代表一切發生 。
the rest of physics is about describing what can happen and what can't .	其他物理學的描述可能發生了什麼事 。
what physics tells us is that everything comes down to geometry and the interactions of elementary particles .	物理學告訴我們 , 一切都在幾何 , 物理學會告訴我們 。
and things can happen only if these interactions are perfectly balanced .	只要這些互動是完美的平衡 。
now i'll go ahead and describe how we know about these particles , what they are and how this balance works .	現在我要告訴大家 , 我們如何知道這些粒子 , 以及如何處理這些粒子 。
in this machine , a beam of protons and antiprotons are accelerated to near the speed of light and brought together in a collision , producing a burst of pure energy .	在這台機器中 , 原子和光線 , 形成了一顆光線 , 形成了一大堆積木 。
this energy is immediately converted into a spray of subatomic particles , with detectors and computers used to figure out their properties .	這個能量被轉化成一種噴射性粒子 , 和電腦用來找出它們的特性 。
this enormous machine the large hadron collider at cern in geneva has a circumference of 17 miles and , when it's operating , draws five times as much power as the city of monterey .	這種巨大的大型鐵粒在大型鐵柱中 , 當它運作時 , 大約有十七英里的速度 , 當它運作時 , 它的運作方式 , 大約是十七英里 。
we can't predict specifically what particles will be produced in any individual collision .	我們無法預測預測特定的粒子會在任何個體中產生 。
quantum mechanics tells us all possibilities are realized .	量子力學告訴我們所有可能性 。
but physics does tell us what particles can be produced .	但物理告訴我們粒子可以產生什麼粒子 。
these particles must have just as much mass and energy as is carried in by the proton and antiproton .	這些粒子必須有大量和能量 , 如同在波斯頓和維爾斯頓的粒子中 。
any particles more massive than this energy limit aren't produced , and remain invisible to us .	任何粒子比這個能量限制還要多大量 , 而我們還不見得出 。
this is why this new particle accelerator is so exciting .	這就是為什麼這個新的粒子加速器非常興奮 。
it's going to push this energy limit seven times beyond what's ever been done before , so we're going to get to see some new particles very soon .	它會把這個能量限制七倍 , 因此我們會看到一些新的粒子 。
but before talking about what we might see , let me describe the particles we already know of .	但在談談我們早已知道的粒子之前 , 讓我描述這些粒子 。
there's a whole zoo of subatomic particles .	這裡有一整個大粒子 。
most of us are familiar with electrons .	我們大部分人都熟悉電子 。
a lot of people in this room make a good living pushing them around .	許多人在這個房間裡有許多人在這個房間裡 , 使他們變得非常好 。
but the electron also has a neutral partner called the neutrino , with no electric charge and a very tiny mass .	但電力和電荷是電荷 , 沒有電荷 , 電荷很小 。
in contrast , the upanddown quarks have very large masses , and combine in threes to make the protons and neutrons inside atoms .	相反的 , 原子的質子和原子之間有非常大的質子和原子 。
all of these matter particles come in left and righthanded varieties , and have antiparticle partners that carry opposite charges .	所有這些粒子都在左邊和右邊的粒子 , 粒子是左邊和右邊的粒子 , 粒子是左邊和右撇子 。
these familiar particles also have less familiar second and third generations , which have the same charges as the first but have much higher masses .	這些熟悉的粒子比較少熟悉的粒子和第三代相同的頻率 , 相同的頻率較高 。
these matter particles all interact with the various force particles .	這些物質粒子和不同粒子互動 。
the electromagnetic force interacts with electrically charged matter via particles called photons .	電力電磁作用是電磁作用 , 電磁作用是電磁作用 。
there is also a very weak force called , rather unimaginatively , the weak force , that interacts only with lefthanded matter .	還有一種非常弱力的力量 , 而非想像力、弱力 , 而非想像力、弱力 。
the strong force acts between quarks which carry a different kind of charge , called color charge , and come in three different varieties: red , green and blue .	強大的力量在三種不同的不同種類中 , 叫做 「 紅色 」 、綠色和藍色 。
you can blame murray gellmann for these names they're his fault .	你可以把murraygellmann這些名字給這些名字 。
finally , there's the force of gravity , which interacts with matter via its mass and spin .	最後 , 重力的力量是重力的力量 , 重力的力量是重力的力量 。
the most important thing to understand here is that there's a different kind of charge associated with each of these forces .	最重要的是 , 要了解的是 , 與這些力量之間有不同的聯繫 。
these four different forces interact with matter according to the corresponding charges that each particle has .	這四種不同的力量互相作用 , 每粒子都有的反應 。
a particle that hasn't been seen yet , but we're pretty sure exists , is the higgs particle , which gives masses to all these other particles .	粒子的粒子還沒見過 , 但是我們很確定存在 , 希格斯粒子 , 粒子會產生一些粒子 。
the main purpose of the large hadron collider is to see this higgs particle , and we're almost certain it will .	大型鐵粒的主要目的是要看到這個希格斯粒子 , 我們幾乎一定會發現它 。
but the greatest mystery is what else we might see .	但最棒的神秘是我們可能看到的 。
and i'm going to show you one beautiful possibility towards the end of this talk .	我會給你們看一個美麗的可能性 。
now , if we count up all these different particles using their various spins and charges , there are 226 .	現在 , 如果我們把這些不同的粒子用它們的粒子組合起來 , 就會有22222 。
that's a lot of particles to keep track of .	有很多粒子可以持續追蹤 。
and it seems strange that nature would have so many elementary particles .	自然會有許多元素 。
but if we plot them out according to their charges , some beautiful patterns emerge .	但如果我們把它們分配給他們的目標 , 一些美麗的模式 。
the most familiar charge is electric charge .	最熟悉的電荷是電荷 。
electrons have an electric charge , a negative one , and quarks have electric charges in thirds .	電子電荷是電荷 , 電荷有電荷 , 電荷有電荷 。
so when two up quarks and a down quark are combined to make a proton , it has a total electric charge of plus one .	所以 , 當兩方夸克結合起來 , 就會產生一個電荷 。
these particles also have antiparticles , which have opposite charges .	這些粒子也有相反的粒子 。
now , it turns out the electric charge is actually a combination of two other charges: hypercharge and weak charge .	結果發現電荷是兩個其他載荷的結合: 「 高速和弱荷 」 。
if we spread out the hypercharge and weak charge and plot the charges of particles in this twodimensional charge space , the electric charge is where these particles sit along the vertical direction .	若我們把這些粒子放在這兩維空間中 , 電荷 , 電荷是這些粒子在兩維空間之間的電荷 , 載載荷蘭的電荷 。
the electromagnetic and weak forces interact with matter according to their hypercharge and weak charge , which make this pattern .	電磁和弱力和弱力互相溝通 , 會產生這種模式 。
this is called the unified electroweak model , and it was put together back in 1967 .	這叫做 「 獨立人工智慧模型 」 , 它在1967年就開始了 。
the reason most of us are only familiar with electric charge and not both of these is because of the higgs particle .	我們大多數人都熟悉電荷 , 因為希格斯粒子的原因 。
the higgs , over here on the left , has a large mass and breaks the symmetry of this electroweak pattern .	希格斯在左邊有大量的對稱 , 來對稱它的對稱性 。
it makes the weak force very weak by giving the weak particles a large mass .	它會讓弱力非常弱 , 使得弱力非常弱 , 使得弱力非常弱 。
since this massive higgs sits along the horizontal direction in this diagram , the photons of electromagnetism remain massless and interact with electric charge along the vertical direction in this charge space .	從大量的角度來看 , 電力和電荷之間的光線 , 電路線的電路線 , 電路線的方向是電路線 。
so the electromagnetic and weak forces are described by this pattern of particle charges in twodimensional space .	電磁和弱力是兩維空間的電磁和弱力 。
we can include the strong force by spreading out its two charge directions and plotting the charges of the force particles in quarks along these directions .	我們也能引導兩條路徑 , 讓它有兩條路徑 , 把它們的條件向方向向方向推向方向 。
the charges of all known particles can be plotted in a fourdimensional charge space , and projected down to two dimensions like this so we can see them .	所有的粒子都可以在四度空間中看到它們 , 像這樣我們就可以看到它們 。
whenever particles interact , nature keeps things in a perfect balance along all four of these charge directions .	當粒子互相作用時 , 自然保持在完美的平衡中 , 自然保持在一個完美的平衡上 , 自然保持在完美的平衡 。
if a particle and an antiparticle collide , it creates a burst of energy and a total charge of zero in all four charge directions .	如果粒子和粒子互相作用 , 它會形成一顆粒子和抗粒子 , 它會形成一顆粒子和抗粒子 。
at this point , anything can be created as long as it has the same energy and maintains a total charge of zero .	此時 , 任何東西都可以用同樣的能量和維持 , 只要它有相同的能量和維持總結 。
for example , this weak force particle and its antiparticle can be created in a collision .	例如 , 這種弱力粒子和抗粒子會在碰撞中產生 。
in further interactions , the charges must always balance .	在更進步的交互作用中 , 荷爾必須總是平衡 。
one of the weak particles could decay into an electron and an antineutrino , and these three still add to zero total charge .	其中一個弱粒子可以變成電子和它 , 第三顆粒子可以變成電子 , 而這些三顆粒子可以變成電子和它 。
nature always keeps a perfect balance .	自然總是保持完美的平衡 。
so these patterns of charges are not just pretty .	這些圖案不僅僅是如此 。
they tell us what interactions are allowed to happen .	他們告訴我們互動如何互動 。
and we can rotate this charge space in four dimensions to get a better look at the strong interaction , which has this nice hexagonal symmetry .	我們可以在四維空間中旋轉這個載荷空間 , 讓它變得更好 , 更好觀察強大的互動 , 這對稱是對稱的 。
in a strong interaction , a strong force particle , such as this one , interacts with a colored quark , such as this green one , to give a quark with a different color charge this red one .	非常強大的力量 , 像這種綠色的互動 , 以一種強大的力量粒子 , 例如這個綠色 , 以一種強大的力量 , 以一種強大的力量 , 以一種強大的力量 , 例如這個紅色 。
and strong interactions are happening millions of times each second in every atom of our bodies , holding the atomic nuclei together .	強大的相互作用在我們的身體中每秒鐘內都有數百萬次 , 緊密相互作用 。
but these four charges corresponding to three forces are not the end of the story .	但這四個載荷 , 不是故事的第三次 。
we can also include two more charges corresponding to the gravitational force .	我們也能包含兩種更多的引力 。
when we include these , each matter particle has two different spin charges , spinup and spindown .	每條粒子都有兩種不同的旋轉 , 粒子有兩種不同的旋轉和旋轉 。
so they all split , and give a nice pattern in sixdimensional charge space .	所以它們都在六維空間中提供一個很好的模式 。
we can rotate this pattern in six dimensions , and see that it's quite pretty .	我們可以在六度空間中進行這個模式 , 看到它非常非常 。
right now , this pattern matches our best current knowledge of how nature is built at the tiny scales of these elementary particles .	現在 , 這個圖案是我們最好的知識 , 圖形在這些元素的知識中 , 形成了我們最好的知識 。
this is what we know for certain .	這是我們所知的 。
some of these particles are at the very limit of what we've been able to reach with experiments .	有些粒子是非常限的 , 我們能達到實驗 。
from this pattern , we already know the particle physics of these tiny scales . the way the universe works with these tiny scales is very beautiful .	從這個模式中 , 我們已經知道粒子物理和這些微小的粒子物理 , 它們非常美麗 。
but now i'm going to discuss some new and old ideas about things we don't know yet .	但是現在我要討論一些新和古老的想法 , 我們不知道 。
we want to expand this pattern using mathematics alone , and see if we can get our hands on the whole enchilada .	我們想要擴展這個模式 , 看看如果我們能把我們的手放在整個國內 。
we want to find all the particles and forces that make a complete picture of our universe .	我們想要找到所有的粒子和力量 , 使我們宇宙中的所有粒子 。
and we want to use this picture to predict new particles that we'll see when experiments reach higher energies .	我們想要用這張照片來預測新的粒子 , 我們想要用這張圖來預測新的粒子 , 來預測新的粒子 , 來預測新的粒子 。
so there's an old idea in particle physics that this known pattern of charges , which is not very symmetric , could emerge from a more perfect pattern that gets broken similar to how the higgs particle breaks the electroweak pattern to give electromagnetism .	因此 , 粒子物理的構想是對稱的 , 沒有非常正確的模式 , 可以讓電磁共振動作更完美的模式 , 讓電磁共振 , 讓電磁共振 。
in order to do this , we need to introduce new forces with new charge directions .	為了做到這一點 , 我們需要介紹新載荷的新載荷 。
when we introduce a new direction , we get to guess what charges the particles have along this direction , and then we can rotate it in with the others .	當我們介紹一個新的方向時 , 我們就可以把它帶到另一邊 。
if we guess wisely , we can construct the standard charges in six charge dimensions as a broken symmetry of this more perfect pattern in seven charge dimensions .	若我們能把標準標準放在六個載荷空間中 , 我們就可以建構標準的標準標準 , 以六個載荷的標準目標 。
this particular choice corresponds to a grand unified theory introduced by pati and salam in 1973 .	這個特定的理論在1973年被巴蒂和薩爾姆在1973年 。
when we look at this new unified pattern , we can see a couple of gaps where particles seem to be missing .	當我們觀察這個新發現的模式時 , 我們可以看到一些小小的粒子似乎被誤解 。
this is the way theories of unification work .	這是一種理論的理論 。
a physicist looks for larger , more symmetric patterns that include the established pattern as a subset .	物理學家看起來更大 , 更具體的形態模式 , 包括基礎的模式 。
the larger pattern allows us to predict the existence of particles that have never been seen .	大型模式讓我們預測存在的粒子從未見過 。
this unification model predicts the existence of these two new force particles , which should act a lot like the weak force , only weaker .	這種模型預測了這兩顆新粒子的存在 , 它應該要像弱力一樣 , 才能產生更大的作用 。
now we can rotate this set of charges in seven dimensions and consider an odd fact about the matter particles: the second and third generations of matter have exactly the same charges in sixdimensional charge space as the first generation .	現在我們可以在七度空間中進行旋轉 , 把這組裝置放在七度空間中 , 並且考慮一個奇怪的事實:第二 , 第三代 , 和第三代相同的載荷空間 。
these particles are not uniquely identified by their six charges .	這些粒子並不是獨特的六個載荷 。
they sit on top of one another in the standard charge space .	他們坐在旁邊的旁邊 。
however , if we work in eightdimensional charge space , then we can assign unique new charges to each particle .	然而 , 如果我們在八度空間中運作 , 我們就可以做出獨特的新載荷 。
then we can spin these in eight dimensions , and see what the whole pattern looks like .	然後 , 看看整個模式的樣子 , 看看整個模式的樣子 。
here we can see the second and third generations of matter now related to the first generation by a symmetry called " triality . "	現在 , 我們可以看到第二代和第三代的對稱 「 試驗 」 。
this particular pattern of charges in eight dimensions is actually part of the most beautiful geometric structure in mathematics .	這個特定的圖案之一是數學中最美麗的幾何結構 。
it's a pattern of the largest exceptional lie group , e8 .	這是最大型的圖案之一 , 8 。
this lie group is a smooth , curved shape with 248 dimensions .	這個圓形狀是248維度 。
each point in this pattern corresponds to a symmetry of this very complex and beautiful shape .	這個模式的對稱是非常複雜且美麗的形狀 。
one small part of this e8 shape can be used to describe the curved spacetime of einstein's general relativity , explaining gravity .	其中一個小部分 , 可以用來描述 「 愛因斯坦公平 」 的形狀 , 解釋重力 。
together with quantum mechanics , the geometry of this shape could describe everything about how the universe works at the tiniest scales .	用量子力學的形狀來描述宇宙如何運作 , 宇宙是如何運作的 。
the pattern of this shape living in eightdimensional charge space is exquisitely beautiful , and it summarizes thousands of possible interactions between these elementary particles , each of which is just a facet of this complicated shape .	這個形狀的圖形形狀在八維空間之間的相互作用 , 可以在八度空間之間的相互作用 , 它們的形狀是非常美麗的 , 它們之間的相互作用 , 它的形狀是非常美麗的 。
as we spin it , we can see many of the other intricate patterns contained in this one .	隨著我們加入它 , 我們可以看到許多其他的圖案在這個過程中看到 。
and with a particular rotation , we can look down through this pattern in eight dimensions along a symmetry axis and see all the particles at once .	通過這個模式 , 我們可以看到所有的粒子 , 看到所有的粒子 。
it's a very beautiful object , and as with any unification , we can see some holes where new particles are required by this pattern .	它是個非常美麗的物品 , 我們可以看到一些洞見到一些洞穴 , 以一種非常美麗的物體 , 以某種角度來看 , 我們可以看到一些洞穴 , 以某種洞見到新的粒子 。
there are 20 gaps where new particles should be , two of which have been filled by the patisalam particles .	有20個葡萄牙的小粒子 , 應該有20個葡萄牙的粒子 。
from their location in this pattern , we know that these new particles should be scalar fields like the higgs particle , but have color charge and interact with the strong force .	在這些新粒子中 , 我們知道這些新粒子應該是像希格斯粒子一樣 , 但有顏色和強力作用 。
filling in these new particles completes this pattern , giving us the full e8 .	在這些新粒子中 , 給予我們全美的八點 。
this e8 pattern has very deep mathematical roots .	這8個模式非常深層的數學根源 。
it's considered by many to be the most beautiful structure in mathematics .	它被認為是數學中最美麗的結構 。
it's a fantastic prospect that this object of great mathematical beauty could describe the truth of particle interactions at the smallest scales imaginable .	這是個很棒的數學美麗 , 可以描述在最小的宇宙中 , 數學美麗可以描述的真相 。
and this idea that nature is described by mathematics is not at all new .	大自然的概念是數學並不是全新的 。
in 1623 , galileo wrote this: " nature's grand book , which stands continually open to our gaze , is written in the language of mathematics .	在1623年 , 在1623年1623年 , 伽利略文字寫了: 「 大自然的本質是數學的力量 。 」
its characters are triangles , circles and other geometrical figures , without which it is humanly impossible to understand a single word of it ; without these , one is wandering around in a dark labyrinth . "	它的角色是三角形、圓圈和其他幾何圖形 , 不是人類無法理解單單一個字 , 沒有任何一個字 , 它的角色是三角形、圓圈和其他幾何圖形 。 」
i believe this to be true , and i've tried to follow galileo's guidance in describing the mathematics of particle physics using only triangles , circles and other geometrical figures .	我相信這是真實的 , 我相信這是真實的 , 我相信這是真實的 , 我相信這是真實的 , 我曾嘗試用三角形、圓圈和其他幾何圖形來解釋 。
of course , when other physicists and i actually work on this stuff , the mathematics can resemble a dark labyrinth .	當然 , 還有其他物理學家 , 我真的在研究這個東西 , 數學可以重新組成一個黑暗的黑暗實驗室 。
but it's reassuring that at the heart of this mathematics is pure , beautiful geometry .	但這數學的確是純粹、美麗的幾何 。
joined with quantum mechanics , this mathematics describes our universe as a growing e8 coral , with particles interacting at every location in all possible ways according to a beautiful pattern .	加入量子力學和量子力學所描述的宇宙 , 粒子和量子力學相互作用 , 由量子力學所描述的 , 我們的宇宙 , 和量子力學 , 這個數學描述我們宇宙中的每個位置 。
and as more of the pattern comes into view using new machines like the large hadron collider , we may be able to see whether nature uses this e8 pattern or a different one .	像大型的新機器一樣 , 我們可能可以看到自然使用的新機器 , 像是大型的新機器 , 我們可能可以看到它的新機器 , 像是大型的新機器 。
this process of discovery is a wonderful adventure to be involved in .	這個過程發現了一種奇妙的冒險 。
if the lhc finds particles that fit this e8 pattern , that will be very , very cool .	如果lhc會發現粒子 , 那會很酷 。
if the lhc finds new particles , but they don't fit this pattern well , that will be very interesting , but bad for this e8 theory .	如果lhc發現新粒子 , 但它們不符合這顆粒子 , 但它們不符合這顆粒子 , 但它們並不符合這顆粒子 。
and , of course , bad for me personally .	當然 , 對我來說 , 對我來說很糟 。
now how bad would that be ?	糟糕是怎麼樣的 ?
well , pretty bad .	嗯 , 很好 。
but predicting how nature works is a very risky game .	但預測自然運作是非常危險的遊戲 。
this theory and others like it are long shots .	這種理論和其他的理論是很長的 。
one does a lot of hard work knowing that most of these ideas probably won't end up being true about nature .	其中一個非常困難的工作知道 , 這些想法可能不會終於自然 。
that's what doing theoretical physics is like: there are a lot of wipeouts .	理論物理學就像:有許多野生 。
in this regard , new physics theories are a lot like startup companies .	在這個領域中 , 新物理理論就像創作公司 。
as with any large investment , it can be emotionally difficult to abandon a line of research when it isn't working out .	隨著任何大量的投資 , 它可以很困難 , 可以讓它無法在工作 。
but in science , if something isn't working , you have to toss it out and try something else .	但在科學上 , 如果你沒有工作 , 你必須去嘗試其他東西 。
now , the only way to maintain sanity and achieve happiness in the midst of this uncertainty is to keep balance and perspective in life .	唯一的方法是保持平衡和觀念 。
i've tried the best i can to live a balanced life .	我曾嘗試過最好的生活 , 可以活過最好的生活 。
i try to balance my life equally between physics , love and surfing my own three charge directions .	我試著平衡我的人生平衡 , 我在物理學、愛和雙手之間的三條路線 。
this way , even if the physics i work on comes to nothing , i still know i've lived a good life .	即使是物理學 , 我仍然知道我生活過了好的生活 。
and i try to live in beautiful places .	我試著住在美麗的地方 。

now it's one of the greatest mysteries in the universe to my parents how i managed to survive all that time without engaging in anything resembling fulltime employment .	這是我宇宙中最棒的謎題之一 , 是我父母在我父母中學到什麼時間 , 不用在任何一場演奏中 。

thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	每五或六年 , 每五或六年 , 她有寶寶 , 每五到六年 , 她有寶寶 , 她有寶寶 , 每五到六年後 , 她有寶寶 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信 , 對於黑猩猩的長期來說 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言很重要 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	隨著大腦變得更複雜 , 我們發現學習扮演了更複雜的演化 , 所以我們發現學習扮演扮演的角色扮演著重要角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕黑猩猩花了很多時間觀察他們的耳朵 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	現在我們知道牠們有能力的模擬行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信 , 這樣我們就能描述這些行為的行為 , 從一代到下一代 , 去觀察 , 那些被視為原始文化的行為 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩不會有一種語言 。 我們談到它 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	牠們有一些非常豐富的韌性和姿勢 , 牠們有許多相似的 , 或甚至是同情形的 , 牠們有非常豐富的韌性和姿勢 , 很多都是相似的 , 或同情 , 甚至是同情形式的 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	牠們也抓住手 , 抓住手 , 把手放在背後 。
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	他們會把石頭丟掉 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩猩的社會中 , 我們發現許多的例子 , 像是同情和真實的親愛 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們像我們一樣 , 他們喜歡我們 , 很黑暗 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	它們是非常殘酷的 , 即使是極端殘酷的戰爭 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些非常激勵的行為 , 大部分部分都在社群中對抗性行為 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	它們是非常大膽的 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	黑猩猩 , 我相信 , 人類和其他動物王國之間沒有鯊魚 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	這是個非常矛盾的線 , 同時 , 我們就會變得更清楚 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我從1960年開始在1960年開始的研究 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	這些黑猩猩 , 牠們的複雜社會生活在野生動物中 , 比其他東西讓我們了解我們是誰 , 牠們在野生動物身上 , 我們有了更多的動物 , 牠們在野生生存的動物 , 我們還能幫助更多 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	很難以發現黑猩猩 , 牠們的棲息地 , 牠們棲息地在世界各地 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這張照片是從空中拍攝的照片 , 它展示給你森林的高地圖 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	那時我在那裏 , 大約十六年前 , 我從公園的角度來看 , 發現在這個地區 , 大約十六年前 , 我發現 , 在這座地區 , 大約16年前 , 我發現 , 在這個地方 , 一個問題來到我在座的海岸 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們要如何拯救這些名黑猩猩 , 當人們生活在國家公園裡 , 那些有名的黑猩猩 ? 」
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多的人都住在土地上 , 都有可能支持 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	數量增加了 , 從法律上升起 , 會增加 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	非常窮的人 , 他們無法買食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	我們稱之為 「 任務 」 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	它是個非常有價值的人們生活在公園裡的生活 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從12個村莊開始 , 現在就在24 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時間來到這裡 , 但它包含了像樹木般的土地 , 把土地放在這些山上 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	可以控制、防止土壤 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	重量的農地 , 兩年後 , 牠們可以再次生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	為了幫助那些村民 , 來幫助村民的水源 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	或許建造一些學校 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 和小組女性合作 , 她們提供了微信貸款的機會 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	我們已經發現了 , 全世界大約有95%的貸款 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦予女性教育的教育 , 提供獎學金給女孩們 , 她們可以完成第二次學校 , 她們可以完成世界各地的教育 , 她們能提供獎學金給女孩們 , 她們可以完成第二課 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭計畫和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	在這個計畫中 , 事情發生了保守 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	重點是 , 在這些24個村莊裡 , 我們都不是在看我們一群白人 , 來研究一大堆猴子 , 但當我們開始計劃時 , 它是塔西班牙人 , 來研究一大堆猴子 , 而不是我們去研究一大堆猴子 , 如同一大堆猴子 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	這是一個坦尚尼亞和村民 , 問他們對他們有什麼興趣 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們對保育有興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對健康有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間開始 , 他們開始了解更多關於保守的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解 , 亞洲山脈的土壤和泥土 , 所以你有這種可怕的土壤和泥土 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	現今 , 我們正在開發我們所謂的 「 更大的生物生態系統 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是美國國家公園的土地 , 把這些非常殘酷的土地帶進去 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	當這些村莊有更好的公園 , 牠們可以在國公園中找到牠們的樣子 , 牠們可以在國公園裡有一百分之二十的食物 。
so tacare is a success .	任務是成功 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們複製它的區域 , 在其他地區的地區 , 和極端的人口壓力 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 在非洲 , 我們已經討論過這幾天 , 大部分的問題都是主要的問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	貧窮很大 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	大量的人住在土地上 , 不管你在土壤開放的樹木 , 你就把樹木放下去 , 把樹木放進去 , 讓它們可以嘗試 , 把樹木放進去 , 然後你把樹木放下去 , 會如何 ? 有些事情會發生什麼事 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	而其他問題不僅僅是非洲 , 而是在我們在地球上所做的事 。
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	你知道的 , 美國人 , 我們需要三個新星球 , 說如果每個人都住在平均歐洲或美國人 , 我們需要三個新星球 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	今天 , 他們會說四個 , 但我們沒有他們 , 我們有了 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	發生了什麼事 ? 我是說 , 問題是 , 我們的確有了 , 那些ted會議中 , 最聰明的是 , 我們的確有了這些ted會議 , 並且我們有了這些ted會議 , 我們的確是 , 地球上有這麼多的能力 , 並且我們有了這些ted會議 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	世界各地的人都在他們做出一個重大決定 , 以後 , 問自己: 「 這決定如何影響我們的七代人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要的決策不是我特別討論非洲 , 但開發出世界主要的決定 , 數百萬人 , 通常都是基於: 「 這會如何影響下一代人 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決定會影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我開始在非洲各地談論問題時 , 我意識到更多 , 許多非洲的問題都可以在非洲的問題上 , 來到非洲的問題 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以 , 我開始旅行 , 談到歐洲 , 在歐洲 , 談到美國 , 和美國 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	到處都是這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	你們知道我在談論污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸的空氣就是我們呼吸的空氣 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球是我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水水是我們要面對的最關鍵的問題之一 , 在這個世紀中 , 水資源都被污染 , 農業和家庭農業 , 都能被污染 , 水源是從過去體驗到的 。
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	溫室會被降低 , 像海嘯變糟的效果 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談到土壤 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們還有其他溫室氣候變遷 , 因此稱之為氣候變遷 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 世界各地的人都相信 , 我們的氣候變遷了 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	全球氣候都混合起來 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	它是窮人的窮人受到影響力更糟 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經被影響了 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在撒哈拉沙漠地區的地區 , 乾旱變得更糟了 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨水下降時 , 它通常會導致洪水、飢餓和疾病 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	數位居民住在一個地區 , 沒有辦法離開 , 因為整個土地都被剝奪了 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以 , 你得到沙漠化的食物 , 再回覆 , 最後的樹木就會被砍掉 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這不僅僅在非洲 , 而是世界各地 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以 , 不令人驚訝的是 , 當我在世界各地遇到許多年輕人 , 他們似乎失去希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去智慧、智慧、智慧、智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	你認為 , 人類心會在非科學領域中 , 來談談它在非科學領域中 , 人類心臟 , 和同情心 , 人類心臟 , 來談談它在非科學領域 , 「 人類心嗎 ? 」 或 「 人類心 」 ?
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	這些年輕人當我跟他們說話時 , 基本上 , 他們說: 「 我們覺得自己有不可思議 , 基本上 , 基本上是沒有人能做的事 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們有了他們的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小孫子 , 每次我看到他們 , 我覺得這個美麗的行星 , 我覺得這個美麗的行星 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	我們稱之為 「 根根和根源 」 , 開始在坦尚尼亞 , 到達97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是象徵性的 , 根源 , 來創造一個基礎 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	射射看起來很小 , 光線可以打破牆壁 。
see the brick wall as all these problems we've inflicted on the planet , environmental and social . it's a message of hope .	看到這些問題 , 我們在地球、環境、環境和社群 , 都是希望的 。
hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數千個年輕人在世界各地都可以打破 , 讓它變得更美好 。
the most important message of roots and shoots: every single one of us makes a difference , every single day .	根源和根源的最重要的訊息是:每個人每天都能做出不同 。
we have a choice . every one of us in this room , we have a choice as to what kind of difference we want to make .	我們有選擇 , 每個人都在這個房間裡 , 我們有選擇 , 我們有選擇 , 我們有選擇 。
the very poor have no choice . it's up to us to change things so that the poor have choice as well .	很窮的選擇也不是選擇 , 而是我們要改變那些窮人的選擇 。
the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根根和根根和根根都是選擇三個計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	它依賴他們在城市或鄉村 , 不管他們是城市或鄉村 , 哪種計畫 。
but basically , we have programs now from preschool right through university , with more and more adults starting their own roots and shoots groups .	但基本上 , 我們有了一些成年人 , 開始他們自己的根源和根源 。
and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每一組選擇 , 三種不同的問題都互相互相互相互相連結 , 並且將這些問題連結起來 。
so one of their projects will be to help their own human community .	所以 , 他們的計畫之一是幫助他們自己的人類社區 。
and then , if they're able , they may raise money to help communities in other parts of the world .	然後 , 如果他們能幫助社區 , 他們就能幫助社區在世界各地 。
one of their projects will be to help animals not just wildlife , domestic animals as well .	他們的計畫之一是幫助動物不只是野生動物 , 牠們的動物也一樣 。
and one of their projects will be to help the environment that we all share .	其中一項計畫是幫助我們共享的環境 。
and woven throughout all of this is a message of learning to live in peace and harmony within ourselves , in our families , in our communities , between nations , between cultures , between religions and between us and the natural world .	深刻在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 。
we need the natural world . we cannot go on destroying it at the rate we are .	我們需要自然世界 , 我們不需要自然世界 , 我們也不能去破壞它 。
we not do have more than this one planet .	我們沒有比這顆行星還要多 。
just picking one or two of the projects right here in africa that the roots and shoots groups are doing , one or two projects only in tanzania , in uganda , kenya , south africa , congobrazzaville , sierra leone , cameroon and other groups . and as i say , it's in 97 countries around the world .	僅僅僅僅在非洲 , 南非 , 南非 , 南非 , 俄羅根和其他團體 , 在烏干達、肯亞、南非、加州 , 南非 , 南非 , 南非 , 南非 , 南非 , 俄羅根 , 或兩個計畫 , 例如我說 , 在非洲 , 烏干達 , 肯亞 , 南非 , 南非 , 俄羅根 , 或兩項計畫 。
of course , they're planting trees . they're growing organic vegetables .	當然 , 它們正在培養樹木 , 它們會成長有機蔬菜 。
they're working in the refugee camps , with chickens and selling the eggs for a little amount of money , or just using them to feed their families , and feeling a sense of pride and empowerment , because they're no longer helpless and depending on others with their vegetables and their chickens .	他們在難民營中營養和雞蛋 , 花了數量錢 , 或只用它們來餵養他們的家人 , 因為他們無法幫助 , 和雞肉 , 去餵養他們的家人 , 因為他們不再無助 , 和雞蛋 。
it's being used in uganda to give some psychological help to exchild soldiers .	它在烏干達提供一些心理幫助 , 來給一些心理幫助 。
doing projects like this is bringing them out of themselves .	像這樣的計畫 , 會把他們自己丟出來 。
once again , they're useful members of society .	再一次 , 他們是有用的成員 。

artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家迪安娜•布萊納•柯恩分享了一些關於塑膠污染在海洋裡的真相 , 我們的生活和一些思想 , 來源自於塑膠污染 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費者主義、全球議題、綠色、海洋、塑膠 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	丹娜•柯蒂:真相對於塑膠污染的真相 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是個視覺藝術家 , 我也是其中一位視覺藝術家 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我和塑膠袋一起工作 , 我在過去二十年間 , 把這些塑膠袋帶回來 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們放進兩個三維的雕塑和雕塑 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	大約在八年後 , 我的工作開始開始融入 , 小小的塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 很棒 。
it's ephemeral just like us . "	它就像我們一樣 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	讓我更進一步 , 我意識到這是一件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	這是一件壞事 , 塑膠會變得更小一點 , 因為它總是持續塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們發現的是 , 在海洋環境中 , 我們發現很多 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	在過去幾年 , 我在過去幾年裡學到太平洋的垃圾和垃圾 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	我最初的反應就是: 「 我的天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須去清潔這東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	因此 , 我真的開發了一台機器 , 一台車船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 和一艘船 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	我的意見是 , 將它帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊 , 把它變成磚塊 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和大家談到 , 在海洋環境中 , 我意識到 , 其實 , 我意識到 , 其實 , 我意識到 , 其實是很小的 , 每天都在海洋環境中生長 , 我發現 , 實際上 , 我發現 , 其實 , 其實 , 我發現 , 實際上 , 我發現 , 其實 , 其實我需要再來看看更大的圖片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的照片是:我們需要找到一種方法 , 來轉換 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要切割到海洋環境的環境 , 每天都在全球性的塑膠 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	所以 , 我也發現我很生氣 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只擔心你試圖想像在太平洋的海洋中 , 我在太平洋的海洋中發現現在有十五個巨大海洋 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	我不只會把塑膠的塑膠放在超市中心 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我到超級市場 , 所有的食物都包裝在塑膠上 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我所有的平均都包裝在塑膠上 , 甚至健康食物市場 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也擔心塑膠和毒素從塑膠帶到我們的身體中 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以 , 我和一群人一起合作 , 我們創造了塑膠污染 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多項目 , 但有些都是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	第一:如果80%到90% , 我們在海洋中發現海洋的海洋 , 我們會發現海洋的海洋中 , 我們發現海洋的海洋中 , 我們發現海洋裡的海洋 , 海洋的海洋是塑膠 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	再回收這些書 , 讓所有人都能回收 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把東西放進去 , 不需要再次思考它 。
what is the reality of that ?	是什麼樣子呢 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 不到7%的塑膠會被回收 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你真的去看它 , 特別是它會被丟掉 , 只會被丟到中國 , 只剩下去 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它被被用來塑膠瓶 , 再一次塑膠瓶的瓶子 , 不用再一次塑膠瓶 , 再一次塑膠瓶 , 再一次塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這對我們來說是個大問題
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另一件我們要去思考的事情是我們在 「 紅色 」 、 「 重新回收 」 、 「 重新回收 」 、 「 重新設計 」 、 「 重新思考 」 第三件事 , 就是拒絕 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	若可能 , 拒絕和可塑膠的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代方案 , 有些是古老的
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在自己現在收集了這些酷的裝置 , 用這些酷的裝置 , 用這些酷的裝置 , 來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道我在做自己和家人 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很簡單是要把你丟掉的水帶到水裡 , 或填滿水、水、水 , 或水瓶 , 不管瓶子瓶 , 不管瓶子 , 或填滿水 。
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我想告訴大家 , 我知道你們很多人都知道這問題在海洋中是很大的問題 , 但這是個問題 , 我們能解決這個問題 。
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們能解決這個問題 , 並教導人們選擇選擇替代方案 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	所以 , 若能選擇選擇替代方案 , 選擇替代方案 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們能拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 。
this demo from pattie maes' lab at mit , spearheaded by pranav mistry was the buzz of ted . it's a wearable device with a projector that paves the way for profound interaction with our environment . imagine " minority report " and then some .	這位在麻省理工學院的 「 少數位置 」 的標準是 「 少數位置 」 的 「 少數量 」 和我們的環境 , 以便是 「 少數量 」 和我們的環境 , 以便是 「 少數量 」 和我們的環境 。
demo , design , interface design , technology	嗯 , 設計 , 設計 , 設計 , 介面設計 。
pattie maes and pranav mistry demo sixthsense	帕特•摩斯和帕特•馬斯和帕特拉蒂•瑪斯和三分之七十六 。
i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我對這個問題很有興趣 , 或許能幫助我們做出正確的決策 , 不論我們是否能進化 , 或開發一個六種感知 , 來協助我們做出正確的決策 , 不管我們是否能做出正確決定 。
and some of you may argue , well , don't today's cell phones do that already ?	你們當中有些人可能會爭議 , 不是今天的手機已經存在了嗎 ?
but i would say no .	但我會說不 。
when you meet someone here at ted and this is the top networking place , of course , of the year you don't shake somebody's hand and then say , " can you hold on for a moment while i take out my phone and google you ? "	當你在ted和谷歌時 , 有人會說: 「 你能否再次拿出我的手機和google ? 」
or when you go to the supermarket and you're standing there in that huge aisle of different types of toilet papers , you don't take out your cell phone , and open a browser , and go to a website to try to decide which of these different toilet papers is the most ecologically responsible purchase to make .	或當你進入超級市場時 , 你就不用你的手機 , 打開瀏覽器 , 打開瀏覽器 , 把你的手機拿出來 , 來決定這些不同的文件 。
so we don't really have easy access to all this relevant information that can just help us make optimal decisions about what to do next and what actions to take .	所以 , 我們無法取得這些相關資訊 , 來協助我們做出最佳的決定 , 來協助我們做出最佳的決定 , 來協助我們做出選擇 。
and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	因此我的研究團隊在媒體實驗室裡研發了一系列的創作 , 使我們能取得這些資訊 , 不用擔心使用者改變自己的行為 。
and i'm here to unveil our latest effort , and most successful effort so far , which is still very much a work in process .	我來到這裡 , 我們最成功的努力努力 , 目前仍有許多成功的努力 。
i'm actually wearing the device right now and we've sort of cobbled it together with components that are off the shelf and that , by the way , only cost 350 dollars at this point in time .	事實上 , 我們已經把這些裝置裝置起來 , 用這些裝置來處理 , 只要花費350美元 , 就這樣 。
i'm wearing a camera , just a simple webcam , a portable , batterypowered projection system with a little mirror .	我是一台鏡子 , 一個簡單的網路攝影機 , 一個簡單的機械 , 一個簡單的機械 , 一個簡單的機械 , 一個簡單的機械 , 一個簡單的機械 , 一個簡單的機械 , 一個簡單的機械 ,
these components communicate to my cell phone in my pocket which acts as the communication and computation device .	這些元件在我的手機中交通通訊和計算裝置 。
and in the video here we see my student pranav mistry , who's really the genius who's been implementing and designing this whole system .	在這段影片中 , 我們看到我的學生的天才 , 他真的是真正的天才 , 設計了整個系統 。
and we see how this system lets him walk up to any surface and start using his hands to interact with the information that is projected in front of him .	我們看到這個系統如何讓他走到任何表面上 , 並開始使用他的手和資訊在他身上互動的資訊 。
the system tracks the four significant fingers .	系統追蹤了四個重要的指標 。
in this case , he's wearing simple marker caps that you may recognize .	在這個案例中 , 他穿著簡單的標記 , 可以辨識出 。
but if you want a more stylish version you could also paint your nails in different colors .	但如果你想要一個更強的版本 , 你也可以畫出不同的顏色 。

phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	伊波菲•羅德里•羅德里•羅德里斯•羅德里•羅德里斯•羅德里•羅德里德•羅德里•羅德里斯•羅德里德•羅德里德•羅德里•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球議題、政治 。
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11的道德:母親找到原諒、友誼 。

and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 我們現在的感覺很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我第一次學到我兒子在世界貿易中心 , 早上9月11日 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他還在直到36小時之後 。

we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們很害怕我們國家會在我的丈夫、土地 , 和我們的家庭 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它時 , 震驚的爆炸是令人震驚的驚奇 , 令人驚訝的是 , 我們的生活中沒有奇怪的震驚 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , 當薩索ui被判定到美國政府為 「 恐怖主義 」 和 「 恐怖主義 」 和 「 公共衛生 」 和 「 公共衛生 」 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過人類權利團體 , 我們和其他受害者的家庭合作 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到一個勇敢的女人時 , 我心想: 「 一個勇敢的女人 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要遇見那個女人當我更強壯 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我還在深深的悲慟 , 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道我會找到她 , 或我們會找到彼此 。

paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	史上 , tedxbrusselselsselselselsels , 他在歷史上看到了這三種主要的轉變 。
foreign policy , global issues , politics , world cultures	外國政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化 。
paddy ashdown: the global power shift	paddown:全球權力轉變 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末期 , 詩人寫了一首詩詩

and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die .
